    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Biletler] AS [b]

    FROM [Biletler] AS [b0]
    WHERE [b0].[UserId] = [a].[Id]) AS [ToplamBiletSayisi], COALESCE((

    FROM [Biletler] AS [b1]
    WHERE [b1].[UserId] = [a].[Id]), 0.0) AS [ToplamHarcama]

    FROM [Biletler] AS [b]

    SELECT COALESCE(SUM([b].[Fiyat]), 0.0)
    FROM [Biletler] AS [b]

    SELECT COALESCE(SUM([b1].[Fiyat]), 0.0)
    FROM [Biletler] AS [b1]
    WHERE [b1].[UserId] = [a].[Id]), 0.0) AS [ToplamHarcama]
FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]

    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Biletler] AS [b]
    WHERE [b].[UserId] = [a].[Id]) > 0

SELECT COALESCE([f].[Tur], N'Bilinmiyor') AS [FilmTuru], COALESCE((
    SELECT COALESCE(SUM([b].[Fiyat]), 0.0)
    FROM [Biletler] AS [b]
    INNER JOIN [Seanslar] AS [s] ON [b].[SeansId] = [s].[SeansId]
    INNER JOIN [Filmler] AS [f0] ON [s].[FilmId] = [f0].[FilmId]
    WHERE [f0].[Tur] = [f].[Tur] OR ([f0].[Tur] IS NULL AND [f].[Tur] IS NULL)), 0.0) AS [ToplamHasilat]
FROM [Filmler] AS [f]
WHERE [f].[Tur] IS NOT NULL
GROUP BY [f].[Tur]
